## Differences
<b>Regular</b>
<ul>
<li>
<details>
<summary>Added between <code>4.8.0-22-generic-amd64</code> and <code>4.10.0-19-generic-amd64</code> ‚ûï</summary>

```c
void cpumask_copy(struct cpumask * dstp, const struct cpumask * srcp)
```
</details>

<details>
<summary>Removed between <code>4.10.0-19-generic-amd64</code> and <code>4.13.0-16-generic-amd64</code> ‚ûñ</summary>

</details>
